The Domain Attribute says:\\n140:    * For example, if the value of the Domain attribute is\\n141:    * \\\"example.com\\\", the user agent will include the cookie in the Cookie\\n142:    * header when making HTTP requests to example.com, www.example.com, and\\n143:    * www.corp.example.com.\\n144:    */\\n145:   if(hostname_len == cookie_domain_len)\\n146:     return TRUE;\\n147:   if('.' == *(hostname + hostname_len - cookie_domain_len - 1))\\n148:     return TRUE;\\n149:   return FALSE;\\n150: }\\n151: \\n152: /*\\n153:  * matching cookie path and url path\\n154:  * RFC6265 5.1.4 Paths and Path-Match\\n155:  */\\n156: static bool pathmatch(const char *cookie_path, const char *request_uri)\\n157: {\\n158:   size_t cookie_path_len;\\n159:   size_t uri_path_len;\\n160:   char *uri_path = NULL;\\n161:   char *pos;\\n162:   bool ret = FALSE;\\n163: \\n164:   /* cookie_path must not have last '/' separator. ex: /sample */\\n165:   cookie_path_len = strlen(cookie_path);\\n166:   if(1 == cookie_path_len) {\\n167:     /* cookie_path must be '/' */\\n168:     return TRUE;\\n169:   }\\n170: \\n171:   uri_path = strdup(request_uri);\\n172:   if(!uri_path)\\n173:     return FALSE;\\n174:   pos = strchr(uri_path, '?');\\n175:   if(pos)\\n176:     *pos = 0x0;\\n177: \\n178:   /* #-fragments are already cut off! */\\n179:   if(0 == strlen(uri_path) || uri_path[0] != '/') {\\n180:     strstore(&uri_path, \\\"/\\\", 1);\\n181:     if(!uri_path)\\n182:       return FALSE;\\n183:   }\\n184: \\n185:   /*\\n186:    * here, RFC6265 5.1.4 says\\n187:    *  4. domain));\\n240:       if(first)\\n241:         len -= (++first - domain);\\n242:     }\\n243:   }\\n244: \\n245:   if(outlen)\\n246:     *outlen = len;\\n247: \\n248:   return first? first: domain;\\n249: }\\n250: \\n251: /* Avoid C1001, an \\\"internal error\\\" with MSVC14 */\\n252: #if defined(_MSC_VER) && (_MSC_VER == 1900)\\n253: #pragma optimize(\\\"\\\", off)\\n254: #endif\\n255: \\n256: /*\\n257:  * A case-insensitive hash for the cookie domains.\\n258:  */\\n259: static size_t cookie_hash_domain(const char *domain, const size_t len)\\n260: {\\n261:   const char *end = domain + len;\\n262:   size_t h = 5381;\\n263: \\n264:   while(domain < end) {\\n265:     h += h << 5;\\n266:     h ^= Curl_raw_toupper(*domain++);\\n267:   }\\n268: \\n269:   return (h % COOKIE_HASH_SIZE);\\n270: }\\n271: \\n272: #if defined(_MSC_VER) && (_MSC_VER == 1900)\\n273: #pragma optimize(\\\"\\\", on)\\n274: #endif\\n275: \\n276: /*\\n277:  * Hash this domain.\\n278:  */\\n279: static size_t cookiehash(const char * const domain)\\n280: {\\n281:   const char *top;\\n282:   size_t len;\\n283: \\n284:   if(!domain || Curl_host_is_ipnum(domain))\\n285:     return 0;\\n286: \\n287:   top = get_top_domain(domain, &len);\\n288:   return cookie_hash_domain(top, len);\\n289: }\\n290: \\n291: /*\\n292:  * cookie path sanitize\\n293:  */\\n294: static char *sanitize_cookie_path(const char *cookie_path)\\n295: {\\n296:   size_t len;\\n297:   char *new_path = strdup(cookie_path);\\n298:   if(!new_path)\\n299:     return NULL;\\n300: \\n301:   /* some stupid site sends path attribute with '\\\"'. */\\n302:   len = strlen(new_path);\\n303:   if(new_path[0] == '\\\\\\\"') {\\n304:     memmove(new_path, new_path + 1, len);\\n305:     len--;\\n306:   }\\n307:   if(len && (new_path[len - The caller is responsible for checking\\n361:  * for OOM errors.\\n362:  */\\n363: static void strstore(char **str, const char *newstr, size_t len)\\n364: {\\n365:   DEBUGASSERT(newstr);\\n366:   DEBUGASSERT(str);\\n367:   free(*str);\\n368:   *str = Curl_memdup(newstr, len + 1);\\n369:   if(*str)\\n370:     (*str)[len] = 0;\\n371: }\\n372: \\n373: /*\\n374:  * remove_expired\\n375:  *\\n376:  * Remove expired cookies from the hash by inspecting the expires timestamp on\\n377:  * each cookie in the hash, freeing and deleting any where the timestamp is in\\n378:  * the past.  If the cookiejar has recorded the next timestamp at which one or\\n379:  * more cookies expire, then processing will exit early in case this timestamp\\n380:  * is in the future.\\n381:  */\\n382: static void remove_expired(struct CookieInfo *cookies)\\n383: {\\n384:   struct Cookie *co, *nx;\\n385:   curl_off_t now = (curl_off_t)time(NULL);\\n386:   unsigned int i;\\n387: \\n388:   /*\\n389:    * If the earliest expiration timestamp in the jar is in the future we can\\n390:    * skip scanning the whole jar and instead exit early as there won't be any\\n391:    * cookies to evict.  If we need to evict however, reset the next_expiration\\n392:    * counter in order to track the next one. In case the recorded first\\n393:    * expiration is the max offset, then perform the safe fallback of checking\\n394:    * all cookies.\\n395:    */\\n396:   if(now < cookies->next_expiration &&\\n397:       cookies->next_expiration != CURL_OFF_T_MAX)\\n398:     return;\\n399:   else\\n400:     cookies->next_expiration = CURL_OFF_T_MAX;\\n401: \\n402:   for(i = 0; i < COOKIE_HASH_SIZE; i++) {\\n403:     struct Cookie *pv = NULL;\\n404:     co = cookies->cookies[i];\\n405:     while(co) {\\n406:       nx = co->next;\\n407:       if(co->expires && co->expires < now) {\\n408:         if(!pv) {\\n409:           cookies->cookies[i] = co->next;\\n410:         }\\n411:         else {\\n412:           pv->next = co->next;\\n413:         }\\n414:         cookies->numcookies--;\\n415:         freecookie(co);\\n416:       }\\n417:       else {\\n418:         /*\\n419:          * If this cookie has an expiration timestamp earlier than what we've\\n420:          * seen so far then record it for the next round of expirations.\\n421:          */\\n422:         if(co->expires && co->expires < cookies->next_expiration)\\n423:           cookies->next_expiration = co->expires;\\n424:         pv = co;\\n425:       }\\n426:       co = nx;\\n427:     }\\n428:   }\\n429: }\\n430: \\n431: /* Make sure domain contains a dot or is localhost. */\\n432: static bool bad_domain(const char *domain, size_t len)\\n433: {\\n434:   if((len == 9) && strncasecompare(domain, \\\"localhost\\\", 9))\\n435:     return FALSE;\\n436:   else {\\n437:     /* there must be a dot present, but that dot must not be a trailing dot */\\n438:     char *dot = memchr(domain, '.', len);\\n439:     if(dot) {\\n440:       size_t i = dot - domain;\\n441:       if((len - i) > 1)\\n442:         /* the dot is not the last byte */\\n443:         return FALSE;\\n444:     }\\n445:   }\\n446:   return TRUE;\\n447: }\\n448: \\n449: /*\\n450:   RFC 6265 section 4.1.1 says a server should accept this range:\\n451: \\n452:   cookie-octet    = %x21 / %x23-2B / %x2D-3A / %x3C-5B / %x5D-7E\\n453: \\n454:   But Firefox and Chrome as of June 2022 accept space, comma and double-quotes\\n455:   fine. Be aware that\\n476:  * sometimes we get an IP-only host name, and that might also be a numerical\\n477:  * IPv6 address.\\n478:  *\\n479:  * Returns NULL on out of memory or invalid cookie. If the cookiejar has recorded the next timestamp at which one or\n379:  * more cookies expire, then processing will exit early in case this timestamp\n380:  * is in the future.\n381:  */\n382: static void remove_expired(struct CookieInfo *cookies)\n383: {\n384:   struct Cookie *co, *nx;\n385:   curl_off_t now = (curl_off_t)time(NULL);\n386:   unsigned int i;\n387: \n388:   /*\n389:    * If the earliest expiration timestamp in the jar is in the future we can\n390:    * skip scanning the whole jar and instead exit early as there won't be any\n391:    * cookies to evict.  If we need to evict however, reset the next_expiration\n392:    * counter in order to track the next one. Pass in the 'newurl' string\n1497:  * as given by the remote server and set up the new URL to request.\n1498:  *\n1499:  * This function DOES NOT FREE the given url.\n1500:  */\n1501: CURLcode Curl_follow(struct Curl_easy *data,\n1502:                      char *newurl,    /* the Location: string */\n1503:                      followtype type) /* see transfer.h */\n1504: {\n1505: #ifdef CURL_DISABLE_HTTP\n1506:   (void)data;\n1507:   (void)newurl;\n1508:   (void)type;\n1509:   /* Location: following will not happen when HTTP is disabled */\n1510:   return CURLE_TOO_MANY_REDIRECTS;\n1511: #else\n1512: \n1513:   /* Location: redirect */\n1514:   bool disallowport = FALSE;\n1515:   bool reachedmax = FALSE;\n1516:   CURLUcode uc;\n1517: \n1518:   DEBUGASSERT(type != FOLLOW_NONE);\n1519: \n1520:   if(type != FOLLOW_FAKE)\n1521:     data->state.requests++; /* count all real follows */\n1522:   if(type == FOLLOW_REDIR) {\n1523:     if((data->set.maxredirs != -1) &&\n1524:        (data->state.followlocation >= data->set.maxredirs)) {\n1525:       reachedmax = TRUE;\n1526:       type = FOLLOW_FAKE; /* switch to fake to store the would-be-redirected\n1527:                              to URL */\n1528:     }\n1529:     else {\n1530:       data->state.followlocation++; /* count redirect-followings, including\n1531:                                        auth reloads */\n1532: \n1533:       if(data->set.http_auto_referer) {\n1534:         CURLU *u;\n1535:         char *referer = NULL;\n1536: \n1537:         /* We are asked to automatically set the previous URL as the referer\n1538:            when we get the next URL. We pick the ->url field, which may or may\n1539:            not be 100% correct */\n1540: \n1541:         if(data->state.referer_alloc) {\n1542:           Curl_safefree(data->state.referer);\n1543:           data->state.referer_alloc = FALSE;\n1544:         }\n1545: \n1546:         /* Make a copy of the URL without credentials and fragment */\n1547:         u = curl_url();\n1548:         if(!u)\n1549:           return CURLE_OUT_OF_MEMORY;\n1550: \n1551:         uc = curl_url_set(u, CURLUPART_URL, data->state.url, 0);\n1552:         if(!uc)\n1553:           uc = curl_url_set(u, CURLUPART_FRAGMENT, NULL, 0);\n1554:         if(!uc)\n1555:           uc = curl_url_set(u, CURLUPART_USER, NULL, 0);\n1556:         if(!uc)\n1557:           uc = curl_url_set(u, CURLUPART_PASSWORD, NULL, 0);\n1558:         if(!uc)\n1559:           uc = curl_url_get(u, CURLUPART_URL, &referer, 0);\n1560: \n1561:         curl_url_cleanup(u);\n1562: \n1563:         if(uc || !referer)\n1564:           return CURLE_OUT_OF_MEMORY;\n1565: \n1566:         data->state.referer = referer;\n1567:         data->state.referer_alloc = TRUE; /* yes, free this later */\n1568:       }\n1569:     }\n1570:   }\n1571: \n1572:   if((type != FOLLOW_RETRY) &&\n1573:      (data->req.httpcode != 401) && (data->req.httpcode != 407) &&\n1574:      Curl_is_absolute_url(newurl, NULL, 0, FALSE)) {\n1575:     /* If this is not redirect due to a 401 or 407 response and an absolute\n1576:        URL: don't allow a custom port number */\n1577:     disallowport = TRUE;\n1578:   }\n1579: \n1580:   DEBUGASSERT(data->state.uh);\n1581:   uc = curl_url_set(data->state.uh, CURLUPART_URL, newurl,\n1582:                     (type == FOLLOW_FAKE) ? unless permitted */\n1606:     if(!data->set.allow_auth_to_other_hosts && (type != FOLLOW_FAKE)) {\n1607:       char *portnum;\n1608:       int port;\n1609:       bool clear = FALSE;\n1610: \n1611:           return Curl_uc_to_curlcode(uc);\n1636:         }\n1637: \n1638:         p = Curl_builtin_scheme(scheme, CURL_ZERO_TERMINATED);\n1639:         if(p && (p->protocol !=        }\n1644:         free(scheme);\n1645:       }\n1646:       if(clear) {\n1647:         Curl_safefree(data->state.aptr.user);\n1648:         Curl_safefree(data->state.aptr.passwd);\n1649:       }\n1650:     }\n1651:   }\n1652: \n1653:   if(type == FOLLOW_FAKE) {\n1654:     /* we're only figuring out the new url if we would've followed locations\n1655:        but now we're done so we can get out! */\n1656:     data->info.wouldredirect = newurl;\n1657: \n1658:     if(reachedmax) {\n1659:       failf(data, \"Maximum (%ld) redirects followed\", data->set.maxredirs);\n1660:       return We need to perform\n1678:    * differently based on exactly what return code there was.\n1679:    *\n1680:    * News from 7.10.6: we can also get here on a 401 or 407, in case we act on\n1681:    * an HTTP (proxy-) authentication scheme other than Basic.\n1682:    */\n1683:   switch(data->info.httpcode) {\n1684:     /* 401 - Act on a WWW-Authenticate, we keep on moving and do the\n1685:        Authorization: XXXX header in the HTTP request code snippet */\n1686:     /* 407 - Act on a Proxy-Authenticate, we keep on moving and do the\n1687:        Proxy-Authorization: XXXX header in the HTTP request code snippet */\n1688:     /* 300 - Multiple Choices */\n1689:     /* 306 - Not used */\n1690:     /* 307 - Temporary Redirect */\n1691:   default:  /* for all above (and the unknown ones) */\n1692:     /* Some codes are explicitly mentioned since I've checked RFC2616 and they\n1693:      * seem to be OK to POST to.\n1694:      */\n1695:     break;\n1696:   case 301: /* Moved Permanently */\n1697:     /* (quote from RFC7231, section 6.4.2)\n1698:      *\n1699:      * Note: For historical reasons, a user agent MAY change the request\n1700:      * method from POST to GET for the subsequent request.  If this\n1701:      * behavior is undesired, the 307 (Temporary Redirect) status code\n1702:      * can be used instead.\n1703:      *\n1704:      * ----\n1705:      *\n1706:      * Many webservers expect this, so these servers often answers to a POST\n1707:      * request with an error page. To be sure that libcurl gets the page that\n1708:      * most user agents would get, libcurl has to force GET.\n1709:      *\n1710:      * This behavior is forbidden by RFC1945 and the obsolete RFC2616, and\n1711:      * can be overridden with CURLOPT_POSTREDIR.\n1712:      */\n1713:     if((data->state.httpreq == HTTPREQ_POST\n1714:         || data->state.httpreq == HTTPREQ_POST_FORM\n1715:         || data->state.httpreq == HTTPREQ_POST_MIME)\n1716:        && !(data->set.keep_post & CURL_REDIR_POST_301)) {\n1717:       infof(data, \"Switch from POST to GET\");\n1718:       data->state.httpreq = HTTPREQ_GET;\n1719:     }\n1720:     break;\n1721:   case 302: /* Found */\n1722:     /* (quote from RFC7231, section 6.4.3)\n1723:      *\n1724:      * Note: For historical reasons, a user agent MAY change the request\n1725:      * method from POST to GET for the subsequent request.  If this\n1726:      * behavior is undesired, the 307 (Temporary Redirect) status code\n1727:      * can be used instead.\n1728:      *\n1729:      * ----\n1730:      *\n1731:      * Many webservers expect this, so these servers often answers to a POST\n1732:      * request with an error page. To be sure that libcurl gets the page that\n1733:      * most user agents would get, libcurl has to force GET.\n1734:      *\n1735:      * This behavior is forbidden by RFC1945 and the obsolete RFC2616, and\n1736:      * can be overridden with CURLOPT_POSTREDIR.\n1737:      */\n1738:     if((data->state.httpreq == HTTPREQ_POST\n1739:         || data->state.httpreq == HTTPREQ_POST_FORM\n1740:         || data->state.httpreq == HTTPREQ_POST_MIME)\n1741:        && !(data->set.keep_post & CURL_REDIR_POST_302)) {\n1742:       infof(data, \"Switch from POST to GET\");\n1743:       data->state.httpreq = HTTPREQ_GET;\n1744:     }\n1745:     break;\n1746: \n1747:   case 303: /* See Other */\n1748:     /* 'See Other' location is not the resource but a substitute for the\n1749:      * resource. In this case we switch the method to GET/HEAD, unless the\n1750:      * method is POST and the user specified to keep it as POST.\n1751:      * https://github.com/curl/curl/issues/5237#issuecomment-614641049\n1752:      */\n1753:     if(data->state.httpreq != HTTPREQ_GET &&\n1754:        ((data->state.httpreq != HTTPREQ_POST &&\n1755:          data->state.httpreq != HTTPREQ_POST_FORM &&\n1756:          data->state.httpreq != HTTPREQ_POST_MIME) ||\n1757:         !(data->set.keep_post & CURL_REDIR_POST_303))) {\n1758:       data->state.httpreq = HTTPREQ_GET;\n1759:       infof(data, \"Switch to %s\",\n1760:             data->req.no_body?\"HEAD\":\"GET\");\n1761:     }\n1762:     break;\n1763:   case 304: /* Not Modified */\n1764:     /* 304 means we did a conditional request and it was \"Not modified\".\n1765:      * We shouldn't get any Location: header in this response!\n1766:      */\n1767:     break;\n1768:   case 305: /* Use Proxy */\n1769:     /* (quote from RFC2616, section 10.3.6):\n1770:      * \"The requested resource MUST be accessed through the proxy given\n1771:      * by the Location field. The Location field gives the URI of the\n1772:      * proxy.  The recipient is expected to repeat this single request\n1773:      * via the proxy. 305 responses MUST only be generated by origin\n1774:      * servers.\"\n1775:      */\n1776:     break;\n1777:   }\n1778:   Curl_pgrsTime(data, TIMER_REDIRECT);\n1779:   Curl_pgrsResetTransferSizes(data);\n1780: \n1781:   return CURLE_OK;\n1782: #endif /* CURL_DISABLE_HTTP */\n1783: }\n1784: \n1785: /* Returns CURLE_OK *and* sets '*url' if a request retry is wanted.\n1786: \n1787:    NOTE: that the *url is malloc()ed. */\n1788: CURLcode Curl_retry_request(struct Curl_easy *data, char **url)\n1789: {\n1790:   struct connectdata *conn = data->conn;\n1791:   bool retry = FALSE;\n1792:   *url = NULL;\n1793: \n1794:   /* if we're talking upload, we can't do the checks below, unless the protocol\n1795:      is HTTP as when uploading over HTTP we will still get a response */\n1796:   if(data->state.upload &&\n1797:      !(conn->handler->protocol&(PROTO_FAMILY_HTTP|CURLPROTO_RTSP)))\n1798:     return CURLE_OK;\n1799: \n1800:   if((data->req.bytecount + data->req.headerbytecount == 0) &&\n1801:      conn->bits.reuse &&\n1802:      (!data->req.no_body || (conn->handler->protocol & PROTO_FAMILY_HTTP))\n1803: #ifndef CURL_DISABLE_RTSP\n1804:      && (data->set.rtspreq != RTSPREQ_RECEIVE)\n1805: #endif\n1806:     )\n1807:     /* We got no data, we attempted to reuse a connection. For HTTP this\n1808:        can be a retry so we try again regardless if we expected a body.\n1809:        For other protocols we only try again only if we expected a body.\n1810: \n1811:        This might happen if the connection was left alive when we were\n1812:        done using it before, but that was closed when we wanted to read from\n1813:        it again. Bad luck. Retry the same request on a fresh connect! */\n1814:     retry = TRUE;\n1815:   else if(data->state.refused_stream &&\n1816:           (data->req.bytecount + data->req.headerbytecount == 0) ) {\n1817:     /* This was sent on a refused stream, safe to rerun. A refused stream\n1818:        error can typically only happen on HTTP/2 level if the stream is safe\n1819:        to issue again, but the nghttp2 API can deliver the message to other\n1820:        streams as well, which is why this adds the check the data counters\n1821:        too. */\n1822:     infof(data, \"REFUSED_STREAM, retrying a fresh connect\");\n1823:     data->state.refused_stream = FALSE; /* clear again */\n1824:     retry = TRUE;\n1825:   }\n1826:   if(retry) {\n1827: #define CONN_MAX_RETRIES 5\n1828:     if(data->state.retrycount++ >= CONN_MAX_RETRIES) {\n1829:       failf(data, \"Connection died, tried %d times before giving up\",\n1830:             CONN_MAX_RETRIES);\n1831:       data->state.retrycount = 0;\n1832:       return CURLE_SEND_ERROR;\n1833:     }\n1834:     infof(data, \"Connection died, retrying a fresh connect (retry count: %d)\",\n1835:           data->state.retrycount);\n1836:     *url = strdup(data->state.url);\n1837:     if(!*url)\n1838:       return CURLE_OUT_OF_MEMORY;\n1839: \n1840:     connclose(conn, \"retry\"); /* close this connection */\n1841:     conn->bits.retry = TRUE; /* mark this as a connection we're about\n1842:                                 to retry. */\n1912:   if(k->getheader || !data->req.no_body) {\n1913: \n1914:     if(sockindex != -1)\n1915:       k->keepon |= KEEP_RECV;\n1916: \n1917:     if(writesockindex != -1) {\n1918:       /* HTTP 1.1 magic:\n1919: \n1920:          Even if we require a 100-return code before uploading data, we might\n1921:          need to write data before that since the REQUEST may not have been\n1922:          finished sent off just yet.\n1923: \n1924:          Thus, we must check if the request has been sent before we set the\n1925:          state info where we wait for the 100-return code\n1926:       */\n1927:       if((data->state.expect100header) &&\n1928:          (conn->handler->protocol&PROTO_FAMILY_HTTP) &&\n1929:          (http->sending == HTTPSEND_BODY)) {\n1930:         /* wait with write until we either got 100-continue or a timeout */\n1931:         k->exp100 = EXP100_AWAITING_CONTINUE;\n1932:         k->start100 = Curl_now();\n1933: \n1934:         /* Set a timeout for the multi interface. The caller is responsible for checking\\n361:  * for OOM errors.\\n362:  */\\n363: static void strstore(char **str, const char *newstr, size_t len)\\n364: {\\n365:   DEBUGASSERT(newstr);\\n366:   DEBUGASSERT(str);\\n367:   free(*str);\\n368:   *str = Curl_memdup(newstr, len + 1);\\n369:   if(*str)\\n370:     (*str)[len] = 0;\\n371: }\\n372: \\n373: /*\\n374:  * remove_expired\\n375:  *\\n376:  * Remove expired cookies from the hash by inspecting the expires timestamp on\\n377:  * each cookie in the hash, freeing and deleting any where the timestamp is in\\n378:  * the past.  If the cookiejar has recorded the next timestamp at which one or\\n379:  * more cookies expire, then processing will exit early in case this timestamp\\n380:  * is in the future.\\n381:  */\\n382: static void remove_expired(struct CookieInfo *cookies)\\n383: {\\n384:   struct Cookie *co, *nx;\\n385:   curl_off_t now = (curl_off_t)time(NULL);\\n386:   unsigned int i;\\n387: \\n388:   /*\\n389:    * If the earliest expiration timestamp in the jar is in the future we can\\n390:    * skip scanning the whole jar and instead exit early as there won't be any\\n391:    * cookies to evict.  If we need to evict however, reset the next_expiration\\n392:    * counter in order to track the next one. In case the recorded first\\n393:    * expiration is the max offset, then perform the safe fallback of checking\\n394:    * all cookies.\\n395:    */\\n396:   if(now < cookies->next_expiration &&\\n397:       cookies->next_expiration != CURL_OFF_T_MAX)\\n398:     return;\\n399:   else\\n400:     cookies->next_expiration = CURL_OFF_T_MAX;\\n401: \\n402:   for(i = 0; The caller is responsible for checking\\n361:  * for OOM errors.\\n362:  */\\n363: static void strstore(char **str, const char *newstr, size_t len)\\n364: {\\n365:   DEBUGASSERT(newstr);\\n366:   DEBUGASSERT(str);\\n367:   free(*str);\\n368:   *str = Curl_memdup(newstr, len + 1);\\n369:   if(*str)\\n370:     (*str)[len] = 0;\\n371: }\\n372: \\n373: /*\\n374:  * remove_expired\\n375:  *\\n376:  * Remove expired cookies from the hash by inspecting the expires timestamp on\\n377:  * each cookie in the hash, freeing and deleting any where the timestamp is in\\n378:  * the past.  If the cookiejar has recorded the next timestamp at which one or\\n379:  * more cookies expire, then processing will exit early in case this timestamp\\n380:  * is in the future.\\n381:  */\\n382: static void remove_expired(struct CookieInfo *cookies)\\n383: {\\n384:   struct Cookie *co, *nx;\\n385:   curl_off_t now = (curl_off_t)time(NULL);\\n386:   unsigned int i;\\n387: \\n388:   /*\\n389:    * If the earliest expiration timestamp in the jar is in the future we can\\n390:    * skip scanning the whole jar and instead exit early as there won't be any\\n391:    * cookies to evict. If the cookiejar has recorded the next timestamp at which one or\n379:  * more cookies expire, then processing will exit early in case this timestamp\n380:  * is in the future.\n381:  */\n382: static void remove_expired(struct CookieInfo *cookies)\n383: {\n384:   struct Cookie *co, *nx;\n385:   curl_off_t now = (curl_off_t)time(NULL);\n386:   unsigned int i;\n387: \n388:   /*\n389:    * If the earliest expiration timestamp in the jar is in the future we can\n390:    * skip scanning the whole jar and instead exit early as there won't be any\n391:    * cookies to evict.  If we need to evict however, reset the next_expiration\n392:    * counter in order to track the next one. In case the recorded first\n393:    * expiration is the max offset, then perform the safe fallback of checking\n394:    * all cookies.\n395:    */\n396:   if(now < cookies->next_expiration &&\n397:       cookies->next_expiration != CURL_OFF_T_MAX)\n398:     return;\n399:   else\n400:     cookies->next_expiration = CURL_OFF_T_MAX;\n401: \n402:   for(i = 0; Meanwhile, we have to call Curl_read\n447:        to ensure that http2_handle_stream_close is called when we read all\n448:        incoming bytes for a particular stream. */\n449:     bool is_http3 = Curl_conn_is_http3(data, conn, FIRSTSOCKET);\n450:     data_eof_handled = is_http3 || Curl_conn_is_http2(data, conn, FIRSTSOCKET);\n451: \n452:     if(!data_eof_handled && k->size != -1 && !k->header) {\n453:       /* make sure we don't read too much */\n454:       curl_off_t totalleft = k->size - k->bytecount;\n455:       if(totalleft < (curl_off_t)bytestoread)\n456:         bytestoread = (size_t)totalleft;\n457:     }\n458: \n459:     if(bytestoread) {\n460:       /* receive data from the network! */\n461:       result = Curl_read(data, conn->sockfd, buf, bytestoread, &nread);\n462: \n463:       /* read would've blocked */\n464:       if(CURLE_AGAIN == result) {\n465:         result = CURLE_OK;\n466:         break; /* get out of loop */\n467:       }\n468: \n469:       if(result>0)\n470:         goto out;\n471:     }\n472:     else {\n473:       /* read nothing but since we wanted nothing we consider this an OK\n474:          situation to proceed from */\n475:       DEBUGF(infof(data, \"readwrite_data: we're done\"));\n476:       nread = 0;\n477:     }\n478: \n479:     if(!k->bytecount) {\n480:       Curl_pgrsTime(data, TIMER_STARTTRANSFER);\n481:       if(k->exp100 > EXP100_SEND_DATA)\n482:         /* set time stamp to compare with when waiting for the 100 */\n483:         k->start100 = Curl_now();\n484:     }\n485: \n486:     *didwhat |= KEEP_RECV;\n487:     /* indicates data of zero size, i.e. empty file */\n488:     is_empty_data = ((nread == 0) && (k->bodywrites == 0)) ?
